<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  // Ensure script only runs on single posts/pages
  if (!document.body.classList.contains('single') &&
      !document.body.classList.contains('single-post') &&
      !document.body.classList.contains('page')) {
    return;
  }

  // Wait until the content is fully loaded
  setTimeout(() => {
    const faqSections = findFaqSections();
    
    if (faqSections.length > 0) {
      convertFaqSections(faqSections);
    }
  }, 100); // Small delay to ensure the elements are available

  function findFaqSections() {
    const sections = [];
    const faqHeadings = document.querySelectorAll('h2, h3, h4');

    faqHeadings.forEach(heading => {
      const headingText = heading.textContent.toLowerCase();
      if (headingText.includes('faq') || headingText.includes('frequently asked') || headingText.includes('common questions') || headingText.includes('questions')) {
        const section = { heading, pairs: [] };
        let currentElement = heading.nextElementSibling;

        while (currentElement && !['H2', 'H3'].includes(currentElement.tagName)) {
          if (currentElement.tagName === 'H3' || currentElement.tagName === 'H4' || (currentElement.tagName === 'P' && currentElement.querySelector('strong'))) {
            const questionEl = currentElement;
            const answerElements = [];
            currentElement = currentElement.nextElementSibling;

            while (currentElement && !['H2', 'H3', 'H4'].includes(currentElement.tagName)) {
              if (['P', 'UL', 'OL'].includes(currentElement.tagName)) {
                answerElements.push(currentElement);
              }
              currentElement = currentElement.nextElementSibling;
            }

            if (answerElements.length > 0) {
              section.pairs.push({ question: questionEl, answers: answerElements });
            }
          } else {
            currentElement = currentElement.nextElementSibling;
          }
        }

        if (section.pairs.length > 0) {
          sections.push(section);
        }
      }
    });

    return sections;
  }

  function convertFaqSections(sections) {
    sections.forEach(section => {
      const faqsContainer = document.createElement('div');
      faqsContainer.className = 'recipe-faqs';

      const title = document.createElement('h2');
      title.className = 'faqs-title';
      title.textContent = section.heading.textContent;
      faqsContainer.appendChild(title);

      const faqContainer = document.createElement('div');
      faqContainer.className = 'faq-container';

      section.pairs.forEach(pair => {
        const faqItem = document.createElement('div');
        faqItem.className = 'faq-item';

        const questionDiv = document.createElement('div');
        questionDiv.className = 'faq-question';

        const questionH3 = document.createElement('h3');
        questionH3.textContent = pair.question.textContent;
        questionDiv.appendChild(questionH3);

        const iconDiv = document.createElement('div');
        iconDiv.className = 'faq-icon';
        iconDiv.innerHTML = `
          <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="chevron-up"><polyline points="18 15 12 9 6 15"></polyline></svg>
          <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="chevron-down"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9"></polyline></svg>
        `;
        questionDiv.appendChild(iconDiv);

        faqItem.appendChild(questionDiv);

        const answerDiv = document.createElement('div');
        answerDiv.className = 'faq-answer';

        pair.answers.forEach(answerEl => {
          answerDiv.appendChild(answerEl.cloneNode(true));
        });

        faqItem.appendChild(answerDiv);

        questionDiv.addEventListener('click', function() {
          faqItem.classList.toggle('open');
        });

        faqContainer.appendChild(faqItem);
      });

      faqsContainer.appendChild(faqContainer);
      section.heading.parentNode.insertBefore(faqsContainer, section.heading);
      section.heading.remove();

      section.pairs.forEach(pair => {
        pair.question.remove();
        pair.answers.forEach(answer => answer.remove());
      });
    });
  }
});
</script>
